\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
The extern \char`\"{}\+C\char`\"{} version of \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_m_s_d}{MSD}}. May not contain the full functionality of \mbox{\hyperlink{_m_s_d_8h}{MSD.\+h}}. To be used for Python3 (ctypes) binding, as well as any future bindings that require a C (cdecl) DLL. 

\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
Christopher D\textquotesingle{}Angelo 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxyVersion}{Version}
1.\+1 
\end{DoxyVersion}
\begin{DoxyDate}{Date}
2022-\/11-\/29
\end{DoxyDate}
\begin{DoxyCopyright}{Copyright}
Copyright (c) 2022 
\end{DoxyCopyright}
